\noindent
\begin{tikzpicture}[x=1bp,y=-1bp,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt]
  \useasboundingbox (0,0) rectangle (595.20,841.92);
  \fill[fill=black] (249.46,101.54) rectangle (374.09,102.98);
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (512.86,772.91) {{\fontsize{11.0bp}{13.2bp}\selectfont Page | 51~~}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (249.46,83.07) {{\fontsize{16.1bp}{19.3bp}\selectfont \textbf{7. CONCLUSION }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,111.94) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont The Credit Card Fraud Detection System developed in this project offers a robust, scalable, and }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,125.65) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont user-friendly solution to one of the most pressing issues in the digital economy: fraudulent }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,139.57) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont transactions. Leveraging machine learning, particularly supervised classification through Random }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,153.25) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Forest, the system effectively differentiates between legitimate and fraudulent credit card }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,167.17) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont transactions based on historical patterns. By integrating advanced techniques such as Synthetic }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,180.85) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Minority Over-sampling Technique (SMOTE), the project addresses the critical issue of class }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,195.01) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont imbalance, a common challenge in fraud detection scenarios. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,218.55) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont From the early stages of data preprocessing---where Time and Amount are normalized and }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,232.23) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont anonymized features (V1 to V28) are utilized---to model training and evaluation, the system }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,246.15) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont demonstrates end-to-end competency. The use of ROC-AUC, Precision, Recall, and F1-score }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,259.83) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont ensures that model performance is measured not only by overall accuracy but also by how well it }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,273.75) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont handles rare but impactful fraud cases. This evaluation strategy enhances the model's reliability and }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,287.70) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont trustworthiness in real-world applications. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,311.22) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont The deployment of the trained model via Streamlit introduces a practical and accessible interface, }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,325.14) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont transforming the theoretical model into a user-operable system. Users can enter transaction details }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,338.82) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont and instantly receive a prediction, making this tool suitable for integration into customer service }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,352.74) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont desks, financial institutions, and digital wallets. The system's architecture is modular, with each }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,366.42) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont part---from data preprocessing and training to evaluation and prediction---being independently }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,380.60) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont testable and extensible. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,404.12) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont A significant contribution of this project is its educational value. It not only demonstrates how to }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,418.04) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont build a data-driven, intelligent fraud detection system but also serves as a comprehensive case study }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,431.72) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont in solving real-world problems using AI and machine learning. Students and practitioners can build }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,445.64) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont upon this framework to experiment with alternative algorithms, incorporate real-time streaming }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,459.58) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont data, or expand the dataset with additional transaction metadata. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,483.10) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Moreover, the system's documentation, modularity, and adherence to best practices such as code }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,497.02) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont reusability and environment isolation through virtual environments make it easy to deploy and }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,510.70) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont maintain. The use of open-source libraries and publicly available datasets reinforces the project’s }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,524.86) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont reproducibility and accessibility. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,548.41) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Despite its effectiveness, the system is not without limitations. It relies on static, historical data and }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,562.09) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont does not incorporate temporal patterns or real-time anomaly detection. Future improvements could }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,576.01) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont include integrating deep learning models such as LSTM for sequential behavior analysis or }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,589.93) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont implementing unsupervised anomaly detection methods to capture novel fraud patterns. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,613.69) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont In conclusion, this project successfully meets its stated objectives by designing and deploying a }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,627.37) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont credit card fraud detection system that is both technically sound and practically usable. It }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,641.31) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont contributes to the broader field of financial technology by offering a model that balances }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,654.99) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont performance, interpretability, and usability. With further enhancements, the system holds potential }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,668.91) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont for adoption in large-scale fraud monitoring environments, paving the way for smarter and more }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,682.83) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont secure digital transactions. }};
\end{tikzpicture}

\begin{tikzpicture}[x=1bp,y=-1bp,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt]
  \useasboundingbox (0,0) rectangle (595.20,841.92);

  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (512.86,772.91) {{\fontsize{11.0bp}{13.2bp}\selectfont Page | 52~~}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (242.26,83.07) {{\fontsize{16.1bp}{19.3bp}\selectfont \textbf{8. FUTURE SCOPE }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,111.94) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont The credit card fraud detection system developed in this project lays a strong foundation for }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,125.65) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont combating financial fraud through data science and machine learning. While the current version is }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,139.57) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont effective for academic and prototype purposes, there are multiple avenues for extending and }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,153.25) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont enhancing the system to meet industry-scale requirements. Below are several key areas where the }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,167.41) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont project can evolve: }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,191.28) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{8.1 Real-Time Fraud Detection }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,217.22) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,216.51) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,214.71) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Currently, the model processes static datasets. In the future, the system can be integrated }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,228.87) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont with real-time streaming data using tools such as Apache Kafka or AWS Kinesis. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,255.14) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,254.43) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,252.63) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont This will enable the detection of frauds as they happen, minimizing potential financial loss. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,276.50) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{8.2 Integration with Cloud Services }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,302.45) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,301.74) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,299.94) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Deploying the model on cloud platforms such as AWS, GCP, or Azure can improve }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,313.86) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont scalability and availability. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,340.13) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,339.42) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,337.62) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Integration with cloud databases and monitoring tools can support millions of transactions }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,351.54) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont per day with ease. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,375.43) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{8.3 Advanced Deep Learning Models }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,401.35) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,400.64) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,398.84) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Deep learning architectures like LSTM and GRU can be introduced to learn temporal }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,413.00) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont patterns and user behavior over time. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,439.27) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,438.56) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,436.76) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont These models can enhance accuracy and adapt to evolving fraud tactics. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,460.65) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{8.4 Model Interpretability and Explainability }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,486.57) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,485.86) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,484.06) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Adding interpretability tools like SHAP or LIME will allow financial institutions to }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,498.22) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont understand why a transaction was marked fraudulent. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,524.49) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,523.78) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,521.98) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont This can build trust and provide valuable insights for auditing and compliance. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,545.88) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{8.5 Adaptive Learning }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,571.80) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,571.09) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,569.29) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Future systems can implement online learning or reinforcement learning models that adapt }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,583.45) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont as new data is received. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,609.48) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,608.77) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,606.97) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont This will keep the model up to date without complete retraining, improving performance }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,621.13) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont against evolving threats. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,645.02) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{8.6 Cross-Domain Applications }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,670.94) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,670.23) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,668.43) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont The same architecture and logic can be adapted for fraud detection in other domains like }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,682.35) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont insurance claims, telecom billing, or e-commerce refunds. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,708.62) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,707.91) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,706.11) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont With minor modifications in the dataset and features, the model can be repurposed }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,720.06) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont effectively. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,743.93) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{8.7 Enhanced User Interface }}};

  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,230.07) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Incorporating end-to-end encryption, role-based access control, and anonymization }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,244.23) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont techniques can make the system more secure. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,270.26) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};

  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,305.57) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{Summary }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,329.22) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont The future scope of the Credit Card Fraud Detection System is vast. By incorporating real-time }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,342.90) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont analysis, cloud-based infrastructure, adaptive learning, and improved user interaction, the system }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,356.82) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont can transition from a prototype to a production-ready fraud detection engine. As technology and }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,370.50) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont fraud patterns evolve, continual updates and expansions will ensure the system remains relevant, }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,384.68) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont effective, and secure. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,408.20) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont The Credit Card Fraud Detection System developed in this project offers a robust, scalable, and }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,421.88) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont user-friendly solution to one of the most pressing issues in the digital economy: fraudulent }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,435.80) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont transactions. Leveraging machine learning, particularly supervised classification through Random }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,449.48) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Forest, the system effectively differentiates between legitimate and fraudulent credit card }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,463.42) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont transactions based on historical patterns. By integrating advanced techniques such as Synthetic }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,477.10) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Minority Over-sampling Technique (SMOTE), the project addresses the critical issue of class }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,491.26) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont imbalance, a common challenge in fraud detection scenarios. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,514.78) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont From the early stages of data preprocessing---where Time and Amount are normalized and }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,528.46) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont anonymized features (V1 to V28) are utilized---to model training and evaluation, the system }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,542.38) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont demonstrates end-to-end competency. The use of ROC-AUC, Precision, Recall, and F1-score }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,556.09) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont ensures that model performance is measured not only by overall accuracy but also by how well it }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,570.01) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont handles rare but impactful fraud cases. This evaluation strategy enhances the model's reliability and }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,583.93) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont trustworthiness in real-world applications. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,607.69) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont The deployment of the trained model via Streamlit introduces a practical and accessible interface, }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,621.37) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont transforming the theoretical model into a user-operable system. Users can enter transaction details }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,635.31) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont and instantly receive a prediction, making this tool suitable for integration into customer service }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,648.99) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont desks, financial institutions, and digital wallets. The system's architecture is modular, with each }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,662.91) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont part---from data preprocessing and training to evaluation and prediction---being independently }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,676.83) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont testable and extensible. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,700.35) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont A significant contribution of this project is its educational value. It not only demonstrates how to }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,714.27) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont build a data-driven, intelligent fraud detection system but also serves as a comprehensive case study }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,727.98) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont in solving real-world problems using AI and machine learning. Students and practitioners can build }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,741.90) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont upon this framework to experiment with alternative algorithms, incorporate real-time streaming }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,755.82) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont data, or expand the dataset with additional transaction metadata. }};
\end{tikzpicture}

\begin{tikzpicture}[x=1bp,y=-1bp,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt]
  \useasboundingbox (0,0) rectangle (595.20,841.92);
  \fill[fill=black] (248.74,101.54) rectangle (375.05,102.98);
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (512.86,772.91) {{\fontsize{11.0bp}{13.2bp}\selectfont Page | 55~~}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (248.74,83.07) {{\fontsize{16.1bp}{19.3bp}\selectfont \textbf{9. LIMITATIONS }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,111.94) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont While the Credit Card Fraud Detection System offers a practical solution with a solid foundation in }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,125.65) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont machine learning, it is important to recognize several limitations that currently constrain the }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,141.52) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont system’s functionality and scalability. Understanding these limitations allows for informed }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,153.49) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont decisions about future improvements and realistic expectations for current performance. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,177.36) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{9.1 Static Dataset Usage }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,203.78) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,203.07) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,201.27) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont The system relies on a static dataset (creditcard.csv) collected from historical transactions. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,227.30) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,226.59) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,224.79) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont It cannot automatically adapt to changes in user behavior or fraud tactics unless the model is }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,238.71) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont manually retrained. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,262.58) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{9.2}}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (85.97,262.47) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont  }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (89.09,262.58) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{Lack of Real-Time Capabilities}}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (249.22,262.47) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont  }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,288.53) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,287.82) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,286.02) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Although the system provides predictions through a user interface, it is not integrated with }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,300.18) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont any real-time data pipelines. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,326.21) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,325.50) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,323.70) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont This limits the applicability of the model in scenarios where instant fraud detection is }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,337.86) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont critical. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,361.73) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{9.3 Simplified User Interface }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,387.91) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,387.20) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,385.40) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont The current UI is functional but basic, developed using Streamlit. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,411.43) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,410.72) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,408.92) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont It lacks role-based access, data visualization dashboards, or automated reporting features }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,423.08) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont found in full-scale applications. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,446.95) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{9.4 Limited Feature Set }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,473.13) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,472.42) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,470.62) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont The dataset features are anonymized and restricted to V1--V28, Time, and Amount. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,496.65) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,495.94) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,494.14) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Important behavioral or contextual data (e.g., location, device ID, IP address) are missing, }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,508.30) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont which may improve prediction accuracy. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,532.17) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{9.5 No Unsupervised or Hybrid Models }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,558.36) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,557.65) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,555.85) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont The current approach uses only supervised learning (Random Forest). }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,581.88) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,581.17) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,579.37) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Unsupervised techniques such as Isolation Forest or clustering could help identify new types }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,593.53) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont of fraud that haven't been labeled. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,617.40) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{9.6 Imbalanced Data Handling Constraints }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,643.34) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,642.63) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,640.83) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont Although SMOTE is used to balance the classes, it may introduce synthetic patterns that }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,654.75) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont don’t exist in real-world data. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,681.26) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,680.55) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,678.75) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont It may also lead to overfitting if not handled with proper cross-validation techniques. }};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (70.82,702.62) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont \textbf{9.7 No Model Explainability in UI }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (88.85,728.81) {{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont •}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (93.41,728.10) {\textsf{{\fontsize{10.1bp}{12.1bp}\selectfont  }}};
  \node[anchor=north west,inner sep=0pt,outer sep=0pt] at (106.85,726.30) {{\fontsize{12.0bp}{14.4bp}\selectfont The system lacks an integrated method for explaining model predictions. }};
\end{tikzpicture}
